< review>
Since they are one of the few places around still open, I was expecting to pay a lot. However, the veterinary hospital only charged a few hundred (100-400, I forget) for getting my little boy up to date on all his vaccines, tested him for FIV and feline leukemia virus (negative on both!), and most of that cost was for the doctors time. When I went back to get a booster shot for him, they only charged the cost of the vaccine!
Very affordable, fair price. Very kind and professional staff. Would highly recommend!</review>

< review>
A year ago, I moved to Santa Rosa from Nashville where I had a great vet for my two Cavalier King Charles Spaniels, Nugget and Brody, so I did extensive research on the best place in town to bring my "kids." Dr. Krome, Dr Lester, and their whole team did not disappoint. Everyone is always friendly and helpful. The manager, Hannah (also a vet tech/anesthesiologist and dog trainer extraordinaire), has always gone above and beyond to take care of my pups. She even coordinated an after hours visit for urgent lab tests when Nugget was unwell, texted the results to Dr. Krome, and we had a diagnosis and plan in under an hour. On another occasion, the front office coordinators allowed me to pay over the phone and arranged for me to pick up Brody's prescription after they had closed, so he wouldn't miss a dose over the weekend. I am so grateful for this intelligent, hard working, and truly caring team. THANK YOU!< /review>

<review>I have had cats all my life, and been to various vets over the years. So, it is with this basis for comparison that I can say Dr. Krome is excellent.

I was worried about taking Maximus anywhere. I inherited him a year ago, and the previous owner said she had never taken him to the vet. He doesn't like to be picked up, and I was worried about stuffing him in a cat carrier and hauling him away from home for some poking, prodding and shots.

Max didn't like the trip (to be expected), but Dr. Krome and his staff were top notch in how they handled him. Max endured it all (even the thermometer in his backside) with surprising calm.

The surprise for me was the bill, which was lower than I expected. When I read the other reviews, I discovered a 2011 review where a pet owner wrote a long diatribe about rates. It certainly didn't match my experience. And, to be fair, it should be noted that Dr. Krome didn't own the business then, either.

I particularly like the fact that his vet has a special certification for cat handling--not something all vets can claim.

All said, I highly recommend Dr. Krome and Santa Rosa Veterinary Hospital!<//review>< Date>
